The day decided was 11th Nov. We were very excited.',  We began our journey at 7:00am in the morning. We occupied two buses. We were accompanied by 4 Teachers- Mrs. Neeru Puri, Mrs. Jyoti, Ms. Balwinder Kaur and Mr. Gagandeep Sharma. We really enjoyed during the journey. We played games, sang songs. The best part of our trip was the time we spent in t', ...', he bus. The teachers also interacted with us in a very friendly manner. At 10:00 am we reached Virasat\u2013E-Khalsa at Shri Anandpur Sahib. We took our tickets. We were divided into 2 groups. The timings for the first group was 11:40 am and second group at 12:00 pm. Till the time we had our breakfast & refreshed ourselves, we clicked Photographs. Then, at 11:40am we moved Inside. It depicted the Punjabi Culture. We were fascinated by the vast history. From the first Guru of Sikhs Shri Guru Nanak Dev Ji to the tenth Guru Shri Gobind Singh Ji. Each & every aspect was marvellously presented. The Purpose is to enlighten the rid culture to create a sense of superiority among new generations. It really deserves to be the 8th  wonder of the world. We really learnt many new things. We went to Gurudwara Anandpur Sahib. The Place where 10th Guru laid foundation of \u2018Khalsa Panth\u2019. We felt really blessed. We had \u2018langar\u2019 over there. Our next stop was \u2018Fatehgarh Sahib\u2019. It is the Place where young Sahibzadas of Guru Gobind Singh Ji, were martyred. It is a very holy Place for Sikh people. We sat to our journey back to Nabha. We reached Nabha at 6:00 pm.  ',  I thank the IBS management for giving us a chance of golden memories to be cherished all throughout our lives as it is our last year in IBS. It was a great day.
